class=\"row\">\n      <div class=\"large-12 medium-12 small-12 columns\">\n         <h1 class=\"text-center\">AMEN CLINIC'S BLOG</h1>\n         <h2 class=\"text-center\">Fresh insight, up-to-date news and commentary from The Amen Clinics</h2>\n         <div class=\"row post-block-3 post-1\">\n\t                <div class=\"large-4 medium-5 small-12 columns\">\n\t                    <a href=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/blog/women-struggle-add/\"><img width=\"800\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/couple-8x4.jpg\" class=\"attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image\" alt=\"It’s Not Just for Boys: Women, Stop Struggling with ADD Today\" srcset=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/couple-8x4.jpg 800w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/couple-8x4-250x125.jpg 250w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/couple-8x4-768x384.jpg 768w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/couple-8x4-700x350.jpg 700w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/couple-8x4-120x60.jpg 120w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></a>\n\t                </div>\n\t                <div class=\"large-8 medium-7 small-12 columns body-entry\">\n\t                        <h3><a href=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/blog/women-struggle-add/\">It’s Not Just for Boys: Women, Stop Struggling with ADD Today</a></h3>\n\t                        <p class=\"author\"><i>by Amen Clinics</i></p>\n\t                        <p class=\"entry\">Despite being diagnosed much more rarely than men, many women around the world struggle with ADD. While there is no biological evidence that ADD affects boys more than girls, boys are more than twice as likely to receive the diagnosis. This means that there is a massive population of women struggling with untreated ADD; it […]</p>\n\t                        <a href=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/blog/women-struggle-add/\" class=\"button small\">read more  <i class=\"fa fa-caret-right\"></i></a>\n\t                        <hr>\n\t                </div>\n\t            </div><div class=\"row post-block-3 post-2\">\n\t                <div class=\"large-4 medium-5 small-12 columns\">\n\t                    <a href=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/blog/10-ways-help-autism/\"><img width=\"800\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/autism-help-8x4.jpg\" class=\"attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image\" alt=\"10 Simple Ways to Help Autism\" srcset=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/autism-help-8x4.jpg 800w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/autism-help-8x4-250x125.jpg 250w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/autism-help-8x4-768x384.jpg 768w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/autism-help-8x4-700x350.jpg 700w, http://www.amenclinics.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/autism-help-8x4-120x60.jpg 120w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></a>\n\t                </div>\n\t                <div class=\"large-8 medium-7 small-12 columns body-entry\">\n\t                        <h3><a href=\"http://www.amenclinics.com/blog/10-ways-help-autism/\">10 Simple Ways to Help Autism</a></h3>\n\t                        <p class=\"author\"><i>by Amen Clinics</i></p>\n\t                        <p class=\"entry\">According to the&nbsp;Centers for Disease Control and Prevention&nbsp;(CDC), autism spectrum disorders (ASD) are a group of developmental disabilities characterized by communication challenges, abnormal social skills, learning disabilities, and behavioral problems. Since ASD are “spectrum disorders,” they affect each person in different&nbsp;ways&nbsp;and can range from very mild to severe.
